        :param service: Ancilary Chatting Robie class instance.
        :param client_mtmsock: Object to mock client connection.
        """

        childs = robie.childs

            client, MTMClient)

        """
    
        robie = service.robie
        childs = robie.childs
        clients = childs.clients
    
        client = clients['ircbot']
    
        assert isinstance(
            client, IRCClient)
    
    
        messages: list[IRCMessage] = []
    
    
        def _callback(
            mitem: 'RobieMessage',
        ) -> None:
    
            assert isinstance(
                mitem, IRCMessage)
    
            messages.append(mitem)

         .subscribe(_callback))

            clients=['ircbot'],
            plugins=['status'])

            target=service.operate)
